<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成式视频模型虽然视觉保真度高，但在企业应用中存在时间不一致性和严重的品牌错位问题，单体架构难以强制执行严格的品牌约束，经常产生未经批准的品牌视觉资产。

Method: Genflow采用复合AI系统架构，包含两个核心组件：(1) 基于检索的"品牌DNA"提取模块，根据既定企业标识指南参数化生成过程；(2) 对抗性多智能体质量控制（QC）循环，利用评估器智能体迭代批评生成帧，引导生成器模型优化输出，直至达成确定性共识。

Result: 将品牌合规视频生成成功率从42%提升至89%。

Conclusion: 通过转向多阶段、自校正流水线，Genflow为可扩展的企业级生成系统建立了稳健框架。

Abstract: Recent advancements in generative video models demonstrate high visual fidelity, yet their integration into enterprise environments is restricted by temporal inconsistencies and severe brand misalignment. Current monolithic architectures struggle to enforce rigid brand constraints, frequently hallucinating unapproved visual assets. We introduce Genflow, a Compound AI System designed to enforce brand consistency in generative media production. Our architecture integrates a retrieval-based 'Brand DNA' extraction module to parameterize generation according to established corporate identity guidelines. Furthermore, we implement an Adversarial Multi-Agent Quality Control (QC) loop. Instead of a single-pass generation, this pipeline employs evaluator agents to iteratively critique generated frames against the extracted parameters, prompting generator models to refine outputs until a deterministic consensus is reached. By transitioning to a multi-stage, self-correcting pipeline, Genflow improved the yield of brand-compliant video generations from 42% to 89%, establishing a robust framework for scalable, enterprise-grade generative systems.

</details>


### [199] [QuadLink: Autoregressive Quad-Dominant Mesh Generation via Point-Relation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16813)
*Yiheng Zhang,Zhe Zhu,Tingrui Shen,Zhuojiang Cai,Tianxiao Li,Zixing Zhao,Qiujie Dong,Zhiyang Dou,Jiepeng Wang,Le Wan,Yuwang Wang,Wenping Wang,Yuan Liu,Cheng Lin*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: QuadLink是一个三阶段统一框架，通过将点云中的点链接为结构化面来生成生产就绪的四边形主导网格。该方法采用混合质心条件顶点链接模型，先预测锚点（顶点和面质心），再学习质心条件链接，最后通过四边形优先策略组装多边形面。同时引入Tri-to-Quad算子将艺术三角形网格转换为四边形主导训练数据。实验表明该方法在几何保真度和拓扑质量上优于现有基线，并原生支持混合多边形拓扑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从点云生成各向异性的四边形主导网格是现代3D内容创作的基础，但现有方法要么只能生成纯三角形网格，要么只能生成各向同性密度的纯四边形网格，无法有效生成具有连贯边流的生产就绪四边形主导网格。

Method: QuadLink采用三阶段统一框架：1）预测统一的顶点和面质心锚点集；2）学习质心条件链接，将顶点与面质心关联；3）采用四边形优先策略，结合鲁棒的几何验证方法组装多边形面。此外，引入Tri-to-Quad算子通过全局合并选择将艺术三角形网格转换为四边形主导训练数据。

Result: 大量实验表明QuadLink能从点云生成生产就绪的四边形主导网格，在几何保真度和拓扑质量上优于现有基线方法，并原生支持任意n边形网格的混合多边形拓扑。

Conclusion: QuadLink通过基于链接的公式实现了稀疏各向异性四边形主导网格的高效生成，具有连贯边流并支持混合多边形拓扑，无需架构更改即可泛化到任意n边形网格。

Abstract: The generation of production-ready quad-dominant meshes is a cornerstone of modern 3D content creation. Generating anisotropic quad-dominant meshes from point clouds is challenging, as existing methods are typically limited to producing either pure triangular meshes or pure quadrilateral meshes with isotropic densities. In this paper, we present QuadLink, a unified framework consisting of three stages for quad-dominant mesh generation by linking points into structured faces. QuadLink formulates polygonal mesh generation as a hybrid centroid-conditioned vertex linking model: it first predicts a unified set of anchors (vertices and face centroids), then learns centroid-conditioned links that associate vertices with face centroids, and finally assembles polygonal faces with a quad-first strategy guided by robust geometric verification strategies. This link-based formulation enables efficient generation of sparse and anisotropic quad-dominant meshes with coherent edge flow and meanwhile supporting hybrid polygonal topology. To construct training data for this model, we further introduce a Tri-to-Quad Operator that converts artistic triangle meshes into quad-dominant training data via global merge selection. Extensive experiments show that QuadLink produces production-ready quad-dominant meshes from point clouds and achieves improved geometric fidelity and topological quality compared to prior baselines. Our method natively supports hybrid polygonal topology, generalizing to arbitrary n-gon meshes without architectural changes.

### [200] [A Single Atlas is All You Need: Decoder-Side Gaussian Splatting for Immersive Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17002)
*Dawid Mieloch,Stuart Perry*

Main category: cs.GR

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 沉浸式视频传输受限于像素率瓶颈，现有DSDE方法处理复杂几何、视角间闪烁和非朗伯反射时表现不佳，而3DGS传输开销过高且与视频编码不兼容。

Method: 提出DSGS框架，在解码端用前馈3DGS推理替代传统深度估计，从压缩纹理和元数据中优化体积场景，利用有损压缩的隐式低通滤波效应稳定高斯预测。

Result: 在4输入视图的极端稀疏设置下，DSGS相比DSDE锚点获得+5.79 dB BD-PSNR和+0.054 BD-SSIM提升；最大视角间Delta IV-PSNR从17.2 dB降至6.4 dB；有损压缩十倍缩小体积的同时质量优于无损。

Abstract: Immersive video delivery is bottlenecked by pixel-rate constraints, making the transmission of high-resolution depth maps or explicit 3D volumetric data expensive. Decoder-Side Depth Estimation (DSDE) shifts depth computation to the client, but struggles with complex geometries, inter-view flickering, and non-Lambertian reflections. Conversely, 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) offers state-of-the-art view synthesis, but transmitting splats (or their projected 2D maps) incurs prohibitive bandwidth costs and is poorly aligned with standard video codecs. We propose Decoder-Side Gaussian Splatting (DSGS), a framework that natively replaces the depth-estimation stage of DSDE with feed-forward 3DGS inference, optimizing volumetric scenes entirely on the decoder side from compressed textures and metadata. A central, counterintuitive finding is that lossy compression acts as an implicit low-pass filter stabilizing feed-forward splat prediction: compressed bitstreams exceed lossless quality while shrinking tenfold. Under extreme view sparsity (one 2D atlas comprising 4 input views), DSGS achieves a +5.79 dB BD-PSNR and +0.054 BD-SSIM gain over the DSDE anchor while reducing maximum inter-view Delta IV-PSNR from 17.2 dB to 6.4 dB, minimizing the domain shift between transmitted and virtual viewports.

### [201] [Topo-GS: Continuous Volumetric Embedding of High-Dimensional Data via Topological Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17011)
*João Paulo Gois,Luis Gustavo Nonato*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: Topo-GS 利用3D高斯溅射技术，通过无网格体素重建将高维数据投影为连续的2D/3D体积表示，解决了传统散点图存在的视觉遮挡和人工不连续问题，同时保持局部拓扑保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统降维算法将高维数据映射为离散点云，这种离散抽象容易导致视觉遮挡和人工不连续性，无法反映底层流形的连续密度分布，亟需一种能够生成连续体积表示的降维方法。

Method: 将3D高斯溅射重新用于无网格体素重建过程，使用局部几何约束（而非光度损失）驱动优化；通过正交Procrustes目标强制实现As-Rigid-As-Possible先验，并将每个高斯的空间协方差与局部切空间对齐；采用拓扑感知策略，针对1D轨迹和2D曲面分别定制损失函数。

Result: 成功将离散散点图转换为连续体积表示，投影失真表现为可观察的几何变化，同时保持与离散基线方法相当的局部拓扑保真度。

Conclusion: Topo-GS为降维可视化提供了一种新的连续体素范式，有效克服了传统点云方法的固有限制，在保持拓扑保真的同时增强了投影结果的可解释性。

Abstract: Dimensionality reduction algorithms map high-dimensional data into visualizable 2D or 3D spaces, but traditionally rely on a discrete point-cloud paradigm. This discrete abstraction is susceptible to visual occlusion and artificial discontinuities, often failing to represent the continuous density of the underlying manifold. To address these limitations, we introduce Topo-GS, a framework that repurposes 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) to cast multidimensional projection as a meshless volumetric reconstruction process. Instead of standard photometric losses, Topo-GS is driven by local geometric constraints. By solving orthogonal Procrustes targets, the optimization enforces an As-Rigid-As-Possible prior while explicitly aligning the spatial covariance of each Gaussian to the local tangent space. Recognizing that unrolling data of varying intrinsic dimensionalities requires distinct spatial treatments, we utilize a topology-aware strategy that tailors the loss formulation to preserve either continuous 1D trajectories or cohesive 2D surfaces. Quantitative and visual evaluations demonstrate that Topo-GS successfully transforms discrete scatter plots into continuous volumetric representations, where inherent projection distortions explicitly manifest as observable geometric variations, while preserving local topological fidelity comparable to discrete baselines.

</details>

Abstract: We present VoxScene, a novel anchor-conditioned voxel diffusion framework tailored for 3D scene synthesis. Current data-driven layout generation techniques typically rely on bounding proxies or implicit representations, which overlook volumetric structures. This geometric blindness inevitably leads to severe physical collisions and structural entanglement, particularly in densely populated environments. To overcome these limitations, we shift the paradigm to an explicit, object-centric voxel representation. Our pipeline sequentially synthesizes discrete volumetric occupancies conditioned on prior anchors and local context. By exploiting the mutually exclusive nature of discrete voxels, our approach eliminates spatial ambiguities and guarantees collision-free arrangements, even in highly complex environments. Furthermore, the synthesized high-fidelity voxel grids serve as discriminative geometric queries for downstream asset retrieval. Extensive experiments demonstrate the universality of our method, achieving state-of-the-art physical plausibility and unlocking shape diversity compared to existing layout planners.

### [204] [Accelerating 3D Gaussian Splatting using Tensor Cores](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17855)
*Sheng Li,Yang Sui,Yue Wu,Zhuoran Song,Bo Yuan,Xulong Tang,Yue Dai*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: TensorGS利用Tensor Core对3D高斯泼溅进行加速，通过将光栅化计算转化为矩阵运算并引入跨瓦片分组优化，在保持图像质量的同时实现了1.65倍的端到端渲染性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS在延迟敏感场景中渲染成本过高，其光栅化阶段在CUDA核心上执行计算密集型任务，而现代GPU的Tensor Core处于闲置状态。现有3DGS系统无法利用Tensor Core，因为光栅化是不规则的逐像素标量运算，与Tensor Core所需的密集规则矩阵工作负载不匹配。

Method: 提出TensorGS框架：1) 将占主导的光栅化计算张量化，转化为兼容Tensor Core的矩阵运算；2) 引入跨瓦片分组（cross-tile grouping）以提升高斯复用、分摊开销并提高Tensor Core利用率。

Result: 端到端渲染性能提升1.65倍，图像质量无明显下降。

Conclusion: TensorGS成功利用Tensor Core加速3DGS渲染，解决了光栅化计算与Tensor Core执行模型不匹配的问题，为实时神经渲染提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has become a leading technique for real-time neural rendering and 3D scene reconstruction, but its rendering cost remains too high for many latency-sensitive scenarios. In particular, the rasterization stage in 3DGS dominates end-to-end rendering time, during which the renderer repeatedly evaluates each Gaussian's contribution to each covered pixel, making this stage compute-bound. At the same time, modern GPUs provide high-throughput Tensor Cores for low-precision matrix operations, yet existing 3DGS systems execute rasterization entirely on CUDA cores and leave Tensor Cores idle. We find that 3DGS rendering can be executed in FP16 with negligible quality degradation, suggesting a promising opportunity for Tensor Core acceleration. However, exploiting Tensor Cores for 3DGS is non-trivial because rasterization does not naturally match their execution model. Existing 3DGS rasterization is expressed as irregular per-pixel scalar operations, whereas Tensor Cores require dense, regular, and reuse-rich matrix workloads. Moreover, conventional tile-by-tile execution fails to exploit Gaussian reuse across neighboring tiles, resulting in repeated data loading and thus high data movement overhead. To this end, we present TensorGS, a 3DGS acceleration framework using Tensor Cores. TensorGS tensorizes the dominant rasterization computation into Tensor-Core-compatible matrix operations and introduces cross-tile grouping to improve Gaussian reuse, amortize overhead, and increase Tensor Core utilization. Experimental results show that TensorGS improves end-to-end rendering performance by 1.65$\times$ while preserving image quality.

</details>


### [205] [Tangent Blow-Ups for Processing Non-Manifold Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18215)
*Alice Petrov,Mohammad Sina Nabizadeh,Ana Dodik,Justin Solomon*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出"切向膨胀"（tangent blow-up）表示法，将几何数据从流形推广到包含边、角、自交等奇异性的一般空间，通过在环境空间与格拉斯曼流形的乘积空间上提升数据，使奇点处的结构得以恢复，并在此提升域上定义离散微分算子，应用于测地线计算、分割、参数化和曲率估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有几何处理方法隐式假设输入为流形或从流形采样，具有唯一切平面，但实际几何数据常包含边、角、自交、分支结点等奇异性，使得标准方法在这些点处无定义。

Method: 受代数几何启发提出"切向膨胀"表示，将数据从环境空间提升到环境空间与格拉斯曼流形（切平面集合）的乘积空间，迭代此构造可使在位置重合但切向、曲率或高阶接触不同的点分离；在提升域上定义乘积度量及离散化微分算子（梯度、散度、拉普拉斯算子）。

Result: 在测地线计算、分割、曲面参数化和曲率估计等任务上展示了该框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 将几何处理扩展到包含奇异性的非流形空间，恢复了奇异点处的微分结构，使传统方法得以适用。

Abstract: Many geometry processing pipelines implicitly assume their input data is a manifold, or is sampled from one, with a unique tangent plane at every point. Geometric data, however, routinely contains sharp features like edges, corners, self-intersections, branching junctions, and other singularities, rendering standard methods ill-defined at these points. To bring geometry processing to these and other singular spaces, we introduce the ``tangent blow-up,'' a representation inspired by algebraic geometry that restores structure at singularities by lifting to the product of the ambient space and the Grassmannian of tangent planes. After iterating this construction, points that coincide in position but differ in tangent direction, curvature, or higher-order contact become well-separated. We equip the tangent blow-up with a product metric and define discretized differential operators, such as the gradient, divergence, and Laplacian, directly in the lifted domain. We demonstrate our framework across geodesic computation, segmentation, surface parameterization, and curvature estimation.

</details>
